  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });

  <span id="freeText7931364219507114692" style="display:none">The last thing Dawson Black expected was Bethany Williams. As a Luxen, an alien life form on Earth, human girls are…well, fun. But since the Luxen have to keep their true identities a secret, falling for one would be insane.<br /><br /><i>Dangerous. Tempting. Undeniable.</i><br /><br />Bethany can’t deny the immediate connection between her and Dawson. And even though boys aren’t a complication she wants, she can’t stay away from him. Still, whenever they lock eyes, she’s drawn in.<br /><br /><i>Captivated. Lured. Loved.</i><br /><br />Dawson is keeping a secret that will change her existence...and put her life in jeopardy. But even he can’t stop risking everything for one human girl. Or from a fate that is as unavoidable as love itself.</span>

<div id="review_445759216" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/445759216" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/445759216?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer445759216" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14752286264714743510">4.5+ stars!<br/><br/><b> Ok, seriously, this YA series has me HOOKED !!!! Like woah hooked! I feel like I could easily devour ten of these books in a sitting! I’m totally and completely in LOVE!! </b> <br/><br/>K, first off, very important but this book should be read AFTER <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12578077.Obsidian__Lux___1_' title='Obsidian (Lux, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout' rel='nofollow noopener'>Obsidian</a>. I repeat, <b> READ <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12578077.Obsidian__Lux___1_' title='Obsidian (Lux, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout' rel='nofollow noopener'>Obsidian</a> FIRST </b> !!!!! Even though its the prequel, trust me, everything will make a lot more sense if you read it after. You won’t be missing anything, I promise. Just because these events came first, doesn’t mean they should </span>
  <span id="freeText14752286264714743510" style="display:none">4.5+ stars!<br><br><b> Ok, seriously, this YA series has me HOOKED !!!! Like woah hooked! I feel like I could easily devour ten of these books in a sitting! I’m totally and completely in LOVE!! </b> <br><br>K, first off, very important but this book should be read AFTER <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12578077.Obsidian__Lux___1_" title="Obsidian (Lux, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Obsidian</a>. I repeat, <b> READ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12578077.Obsidian__Lux___1_" title="Obsidian (Lux, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Obsidian</a> FIRST </b> !!!!! Even though its the prequel, trust me, everything will make a lot more sense if you read it after. You won’t be missing anything, I promise. Just because these events came first, doesn’t mean they should be read first because the world is introduced in a very different way, almost expecting the reader to already be acquainted with everything so I really don’t think it would make sense to start with this.<br><br>But, that being said, if you have already read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12578077.Obsidian__Lux___1_" title="Obsidian (Lux, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Obsidian</a>, you’ll be sure to love this one because it fills in so many blanks about that world, the back story, the way their alien species works, the structure of their families and relationships, the way their lives are run and the intricacies of their relationship with the government, and character insight too – like what happened in Daemon’s life that made him so outwardly hostile to Katy at first, the way he sort of became the defacto protector and felt so responsible for everyone… this story has a lot of little missing puzzle pieces that help to round out the world we have already been introduced to.<br><br>This is the story of Daemon’s twin brother Dawson. The story is alluded to in Obsidian but never described in detail. All we know coming into this story was that Dawson was very loved and close to his siblings, that he fell in love with Bethany, a human girl, and that one day, they both ‘mysteriously disappeared’.<br><br>OH THE SWOON!!!! I love Daemon. I really do. But oh my Lord did I ever <b> melt </b> over Dawson. He was day to Daemon’s night. Hot, sweet, funny, kind, with an easy smile and a heart of gold. If Daemon was the bad boy brother, Dawson is the good boy.<br><br>He literally just falls hard and falls fast for Bethany. Its mutual and just seriously, completely adorable and swoony. Totally warmed my heart!! But… in their world, while relationships with humans are not forbidden, they are frowned on. Strongly. But Dawson doesn’t care. He’s completely smitten with Bethany and is willing to risk anything for a chance to be with her.<br><br><i> <b> “I want this – I want you… More than I’ve ever wanted anything.. I want to be with you.” </b></i> <br><br>As the story progressed, my heart started to clench up and the anticipation built cuz I knew where the story was headed. I was so lost in the beautiful swoon of their relationship, I didn’t want anything to happen to them. They were just too freaking perfect and happy! You know that feeling you get sometimes when you just want to pluck a couple out of their little nightmare and throw them on a happy little island together forever, yeah, I totally got that here.<br><br>It was heartbreaking watching these guys fight so hard for just a chance to be a normal couple in love. Not judged or hindered by the rules of their species.<br><br><i> <b> “Nothing else mattered except the girl he cradled to him.” </b></i> <br><br>Gah!! They were just so beautiful and innocent and in love and I just wanted them to be happy *clutches heart* GURK!!! I <i> need </i> to read more in this series! I need them to get their HEA!<br><br>The ending left me totally hanging and desperate for more!!! But, don’t worry, its a cliffhanger you should read anyways, because we already know they are “missing” from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12578077.Obsidian__Lux___1_" title="Obsidian (Lux, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Obsidian</a>… I’m sure their story will be dealt with as the series goes on and I can’t WAIT for it to happen!!<br><br>Like I said: <b> Totally. Freaking. HOOKED </b> !!!!<br><br>CASTING (see pics above and below)<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396091i/763250._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396091i/763251._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8166711782573951467"><b>*Initial thoughts after reading:</b><br/><br/>Oh god, I think I might cry. This was so heartbreaking. But this gave light and more understanding about Daemon's attitude and actions towards Katy in Obsidian. If I could just jumped into the story and help them, I really would. Haha! I have so many theories coming up on my mind now and I'm also so in the mood to re-read Obsidian! <br/><br/><br/><b>*Final Thoughts:</b> (This went more like my review for both Shadows and my second round of Obsidian. Teehee!)<br/><br/>This was a wonderful and hea</span>
  <span id="freeText8166711782573951467" style="display:none"><b>*Initial thoughts after reading:</b><br /><br />Oh god, I think I might cry. This was so heartbreaking. But this gave light and more understanding about Daemon's attitude and actions towards Katy in Obsidian. If I could just jumped into the story and help them, I really would. Haha! I have so many theories coming up on my mind now and I'm also so in the mood to re-read Obsidian! <br /><br /><br /><b>*Final Thoughts:</b> (This went more like my review for both Shadows and my second round of Obsidian. Teehee!)<br /><br />This was a wonderful and heart wrenching story. I loved that I was able to get to know Dawson and Bethany and their tragic love story. And though it ended pretty sad there were parts I had definitely enjoyed, especially those times Dawson and Bethany had been together. It was lovely, sweet and definitely heartwarming. Dawson's relationship with his siblings was utterly beautiful too. I saw how much the three of them cared for each other. And of course, this book has definitely helped me understand Daemon's character and answer the questions I had about him in Obsidian. I now understood why he was such a jerk to Katy and why he was so reluctant to her when it was pretty obvious that he like her too. <br /><br />And speaking of Obsidian, I was serious when I said I was so in the mood to re-read it, so yeah, I did. And yes, I still enjoyed it and still left me as high as I was the first time I read it. It was also funny to see how Daemon ate almost everything he said about his brother doing 'stupid' things. Seeing him do almost the same things his brother did and much more (and I would say it was really way more entertaining actually) was just really amusing. Anyway, I find most of the things that happened way clearer now. Theories were popping up on my mind and I noticed a lot of things now that I've read Shadows too. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Well, things like in Shadows, when Dawson switched to his Luxen form he cannot speak to Bethany because she wouldn't be able to understand him. But in Obsidian, when Daemon switched to his true form he was able to speak to Katy and Katy did hear him in her mind. Making me think that there is definitely something special about Katy. To support that, there was also this thing when Katy passed out the first time Daemon used his power near her to scare off the bear. Daemon said that he didn't know why she passed out and that she was a human so it shouldn't have affected her like that. And of course the last part, the things that happened in the field; the power from Dee and Dawson she seemed to absorb and the power surge she used to kill the Arum. And then the healing thing Daemon did to Katy and made them sort of connected, like they became the other half of each other. Which I'm pretty sure was the same thing Dawson did to Bethany. But something happened to Bethany when Dawson fought, it was like what happened to the other affects the other one too. I wonder if the same thing will happen to Daemon and Katy too. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Oh well, those were just my freaking theories and you don't have to believe me. Haha! I'm just having a major Obsidian obsession streak right now. But it was amusing to entertain thoughts like that. <br /><br />And yes, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[after reading Shadows then Obsidian again and those teasers of Onyx and parts of Deamon's pov from Obsidian posted in Jennifer's blog, I am very much convinced that Daemon is madly, deeply, irrevocably, and irresistibly (cr. for the adverbs <a href="http://jenniferarmentrout.blogspot.com/2012/02/onyx-teaser.html" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a>) in love with Katy!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> You don't have to agree with me but I really like to believed that. God, I'm so obsessed. LoL! I so need Onyx now! But I have no choice but to wait. T.T <br /><br /><br /><b>*Pre-reading Thoughts:</b><br /><br />Oh wait. I just saw the blurb of Onyx and I have this theory that Bethany or Dawson are not yet really dead. Waahhh! Really, there's something more going on! Argh~!I need these books now. :DDD<br />------<br />Awww. Its just sad we already know that Bethany and Dawson didn't have a happy ending. :(( But still, Imma read this! :DD <br /><br />This review is also posted at <a href="http://bookoverdose.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Book Overdose</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1683816847160103427">The tragic story of Luxen Dawson Black and human Bethany Williams. <br/>I have already read the main books in the series, so I knew how this novel ends. Still it was nice seeing Dawson and Bethany falling in love no matter their cultural differences and the negative comments and actions by their family and friends.<br/><br/>Dawson is a sensitive sweetheart and he absolutely knows what he wants.<br/>Bethany is quite nice.   <span id="freeText1683816847160103427" style="display:none">The tragic story of Luxen Dawson Black and human Bethany Williams. <br />I have already read the main books in the series, so I knew how this novel ends. Still it was nice seeing Dawson and Bethany falling in love no matter their cultural differences and the negative comments and actions by their family and friends.<br /><br />Dawson is a sensitive sweetheart and he absolutely knows what he wants.<br />Bethany is quite nice. The book made me understand her better. She is ready to fight for her love.<br /><br />Daemon is the old grumpy self before he meets Katy and realises that humans are not that bad. Evil laugh here because I know what will happen to him and how much he will change.<br /><br />Probably if you have read the next books, you will feel sorry for characters that won't have much future left. There will be glimpses of most of the main characters of the next books.<br /><br />If you haven't read the next books, expect a huge cliff-hanger in the end. And you will be probably be hooked. <br />Otherwise you know how this continues :)<br /></span>

<div id="review_398372579" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/398372579" />
    <a title="Steph Sinclair" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4642710-steph-sinclair"><img alt="Steph Sinclair" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1457555690p2/4642710.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/398372579?book_show_action=true">Aug 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Steph Sinclair" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Steph Sinclair" href="/user/show/4642710-steph-sinclair">Steph Sinclair</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Lux fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=entangled">entangled</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=it-wasn-t-all-that-but-enjoyable">it-wasn-t-all-that-but-enjoyable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=2012-reads">2012-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=i-blame-twilight">i-blame-twilight</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=cool-author">cool-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=aliens">aliens</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=2012-release">2012-release</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer398372579" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14611050419613647934"><br/>Actual rating: 3.5 stars<br/><br/>Usually I don't like reading novellas. I find that I have a harder time connecting with the characters with such few pages. So I was surprised that by the time I read the last page of <em>Shadows</em> I found myself missing Dawson and Bethany. Perhaps it's because I devoured <em>Shadows</em> right after completing <em>Obsidian.</em> I'm not sure. Or maybe it's because despite Dawson and Bethany's absence thus far in the series, I can still feel that they play a much bigger role than perviously real</span>
  <span id="freeText14611050419613647934" style="display:none"><br />Actual rating: 3.5 stars<br /><br />Usually I don't like reading novellas. I find that I have a harder time connecting with the characters with such few pages. So I was surprised that by the time I read the last page of <em>Shadows</em> I found myself missing Dawson and Bethany. Perhaps it's because I devoured <em>Shadows</em> right after completing <em>Obsidian.</em> I'm not sure. Or maybe it's because despite Dawson and Bethany's absence thus far in the series, I can still feel that they play a much bigger role than perviously realized. Whatever the case, I found this novella to be entirely bittersweet.<br /><br />If there is one thing that I take away from reading <em>Shadows</em> it's the reasons behind Daemon's interactions with Katy in <em>Obsidian.</em> Don't get me wrong. That doesn't make his actions okay in any shape or form. But it does give the reader better insight. Basically, it's nice to know Daemon wasn't just being a complete jackass just for the hell of it (though, I do think he enjoyed tormenting Katy at times and she him). What's interesting was seeing the almost the exact same events that happened with Daemon also happening with Dawson; something Daemon tried very hard to prevent.<br /><br />Going into the novella, I already knew the general story behind what happened to Dawson and Bethany since it's referenced a bit in <em>Obsidian,</em> but to actually see it play out was a different story. Dawson is the kinder twin of the Black family, so it was relatively easy to grow attached to him and root for his determination at staying with Bethany despite the obstacles in their relationship. Unfortunately, I didn't have the same feelings for Bethany as I did Katy. She wasn't a bad character and I didn't dislike her, but I don't feel I got a good feel for her. I think it's because most of the events were focused around Dawson than Bethany. And not to mention I was still riding my "Katy high" when I dived right into <em>Shadows.</em> I did like Dawson and Bethany together.  And I usually don't like "love at first sight" stories, but there wasn't any insta-love to be found, just instant attraction that later turned into something more, which is perfectly realistic.<br /><br />If fans are looking for a more action packed story, this one probably isn't it since it does focus mostly on Dawson and Bethany's first meeting to their getting-to-know-you's and dates. It's a much slower paced book than its processor and less witty. I thought that was appropriate considering the novella carried a certain level of foreboding from the first page that demanded seriousness. All throughout the novel you are watching them go through the motions, attempting the impossible, all the while heading for the inevitable. I wanted to reach out and tell Dawson to not go to that movie theatre that night, but alas, the book was already written. *sigh*<br /><br />All in all, this was a very good novella and I will definitely be continuing with the rest of the series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14611050419613647934" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="~Tina~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2594672-tina"><img alt="~Tina~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1411474324p2/2594672.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/245319253?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~Tina~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~Tina~" href="/user/show/2594672-tina">~Tina~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer245319253" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6783512174237014610">*drools at the cover* <a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=ifbn2e' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/61983.gif' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>For the love of all Aliens! I loved this book!!<br/><br/>For those of you who know me already know that I'm a HUGE fan of Jennifer L. Armentrout. She is such a brilliant author and I simply can't get enough of her stories.<br/><br/>I've been looking forward to <b>Shadows</b> ever since I found out it was coming our way. Not only was I thrilled to see Daemon and Dee again, but I've always been mighty curious about Dawson Black who fell in love with his human girl, Bethany Williams. <br/>This is his sto</span>
  <span id="freeText6783512174237014610" style="display:none">*drools at the cover* <a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=ifbn2e" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/61983.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For the love of all Aliens! I loved this book!!<br><br>For those of you who know me already know that I'm a HUGE fan of Jennifer L. Armentrout. She is such a brilliant author and I simply can't get enough of her stories.<br><br>I've been looking forward to <b>Shadows</b> ever since I found out it was coming our way. Not only was I thrilled to see Daemon and Dee again, but I've always been mighty curious about Dawson Black who fell in love with his human girl, Bethany Williams. <br>This is his story. Her story. Stupid, irresistible and in love. <br>Just the way it's suppose to be....<br><br>Dawson and Daemon might be identical twins, but they are so different in personality. Daemon is just as intense, edgy and obnoxious in this book as much as he was in <i>Obsidian</i>, but I finally see the why's and feel like I understand him just a little bit better now. <br>Dawson is warm and kind and infectiously good. But just like his brother he's got a temper and it was a real treat to see him unleash it. Just wow! The way he feels about Bethany is so raw and real. I loved those moments between them. It never felt fake or even rushed, it just felt completely natural. I also really loved how much Dawson and Daemon love their sister Dee. Some of those conversations had me laughing out loud while other times I just wanted to hug them.<br>It was also good to see Adam, Andrew and Ash in this one. Overall, it was just nice to get to know these characters on a different level. <br><br>For anyone who has already read Obsidian, knows what happened to Dawson, so I don't think it's much of a spoiler when I say that it was hard to read the last two chapters and very sad. I'm still clinging to hope. And that's all I'm gonna say about that.<br><br>Bottom line, I loved this book. Yes, this was a novella, but that's the beauty of Jennifer's books, it never feels that way. I just totally lose myself, done to quickly and always wanting more.<br>I'm thrilled and thankful that she gave us this glimpse into Dawson and Bethany's world. It was beautiful and so very very bittersweet. It was a story that needed to be told to get a better understanding of the first book and future books to come. Also, this only increases my anticipation for Onyx to a madding level, but I'll take what I can get. For now;)<br><br>This is a must read for fans of the Lux series! I absolutely missed this world and it felt amazing coming back to it even for a short while.<br><br>MORE!!!<br><br>(Thanks to Entangled Publishing for sending me a copy!)</span>
  <a data-text-id="6783512174237014610" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1595268441" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1595268441" />
    <a title="Emer (A Little Haze)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4629647-emer-a-little-haze"><img alt="Emer (A Little Haze)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589390599p2/4629647.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1595268441?book_show_action=true">Mar 30, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emer (A Little Haze)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emer (A Little Haze)" href="/user/show/4629647-emer-a-little-haze">Emer (A Little Haze)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=2stars">2stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=novellas">novellas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=trashtastic">trashtastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=read2016">read2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1595268441" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9864226449203031356">Oh I am so disappointed by this prequel novella to the Lux series… although I guess I should not be surprised! I was always kinda nervous about reading this and sadly it seems my fears have come to fruition. <br/><br/><br/>This story focuses on Dawson and Bethany… who are a cute couple… but they are <b>no match</b> for Daemon and Katy!! <br/>Where Damon and Katy are all prickly at the start of their relationship and zinging with chemistry…and with banter to die for….oh the banter…. <b>*sighs*</b>…. <br/>Well Dawson and Bethany… they </span>
  <span id="freeText9864226449203031356" style="display:none">Oh I am so disappointed by this prequel novella to the Lux series… although I guess I should not be surprised! I was always kinda nervous about reading this and sadly it seems my fears have come to fruition. <br /><br /><br />This story focuses on Dawson and Bethany… who are a cute couple… but they are <b>no match</b> for Daemon and Katy!! <br />Where Damon and Katy are all prickly at the start of their relationship and zinging with chemistry…and with banter to die for….oh the banter…. <b>*sighs*</b>…. <br />Well Dawson and Bethany… they are all doe eyed and insta-love and 'you’re sweet and I’m sweet! And you’re pretty and I’m pretty!!! So let’s be sweet and pretty together and love each other until the end of time'………YAWN! <br />Okay they made a lovely couple and they shared some very lovely moments... but all in all the evolution of their relationship just fell a little flat for me. I guess the author felt she had to rush the development of their togetherness from first attraction to full on head over heels life partners because the story had to be short. The brevity of this novella definitely did not work for me. <br /><br /><br />The only time this novella was interesting was when Daemon featured… he just <b>
  <i>IS</i>
</b> the more interesting twin. Whenever he featured there was just more<i> **pop** </i>to the story, he has <b>ALL</b> the best lines!! Face it, the boy has got charisma! He is more complex as a character, has shades of both light and dark...and just knows how to steal a scene. So basically this story needed more Daemon!!!! <br />Although I could just say that about any aspect of anything these days. Life needs more Daemon Black!!! LOL<br /><br /><br />And Bethany versus Katy... It's very similar. Katy has backbone, spunk, bite! She may not always make wise decisions but at least she demands attention of the reader. Bethany...she's just nice! And in books nice so often equates to dull... sorry Bethany! This story really missed Katy's presence. <br /><br /><br />This novella is supposed to be a prequel to Obsidian; it is given the number 0.5 in the series… I absolutely <b>do not</b> think that this should be read before Obsidian. Or even Onyx or Opal!! It just ruins the whole mystique of the alien world, of their powers, …and just gives hints as to what may lie ahead. It is just too spoilery!!! So best enjoyed at the end of the series I feel, as a sort of retrospective to how it all began… although I really would only recommend this book to die-hard Lux fans. There is not much to be gained from reading it.<br /><br /><br />Sadly this left me underwhelmed… but at least I have my happy memories of the main books!<br /><b>Two stars</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9864226449203031356" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_248996309" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/248996309" />
    <a title="Rachael Wade" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5369812-rachael-wade"><img alt="Rachael Wade" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1383666913p2/5369812.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/248996309?book_show_action=true">Dec 19, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachael Wade" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachael Wade" href="/user/show/5369812-rachael-wade">Rachael Wade</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5369812-rachael-wade?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5369812-rachael-wade?shelf=crack-books">crack-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer248996309" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12318341448167628941"><br/><b>Kimmy turned on the girl, about to pull a Linda Blair, no doubt.</b><br/><br/>Okay, so forgive me in advance if this review is completely all over the place and disjointed...but that's what Armentrout's writing does to me. She is positively my favorite YA author as of late, and along with adult romance author E.L. James, she is the only one who can elicit such a strong reaction from me when I read her work. I've said it before, and I'll say it again...the woman has mad skills. Not to mention the kind of humor</span>
  <span id="freeText12318341448167628941" style="display:none"><br /><b>Kimmy turned on the girl, about to pull a Linda Blair, no doubt.</b><br /><br />Okay, so forgive me in advance if this review is completely all over the place and disjointed...but that's what Armentrout's writing does to me. She is positively my favorite YA author as of late, and along with adult romance author E.L. James, she is the only one who can elicit such a strong reaction from me when I read her work. I've said it before, and I'll say it again...the woman has mad skills. Not to mention the kind of humor I love (see the one liner above. Yeah. That's just one of the many hilarious zingers I love.)<br /><br />For those of us who have started reading the Lux series, Shadows is a welcome detour while waiting anxiously for Onyx, book 2 of the series. But it's also completely bittersweet from start to finish, because...well, you have an idea of where it's going after reading Obsidian, book 1.<br /><br />That being said, for Daemon fans, Dawson is a heartbreaking and swoon-worthy character that gives Daemon a run for his money. Granted, he's the polar opposite of Daemon, so there is plenty to love about each of the brothers. I won't give away any spoilers, but I'll tell you right now that I was flipping the pages so fast my mind could not keep up. Dawson and Bethany's story is so sweet and passionate, and the sexual tension can be cut with a knife. I was cringing when they were in danger, sighing like a lovesick teenager when they made out, and lighting up with "aha!" moments as the story unfolded because this installment reveals so much about why Daemon is the way he is and it just made me understand the family so much more.<br /><br />The author really understands the key ingredients to a fantastic YA romance: swoon-worthy guys, realistic heroines, wistful romance, action, and humor. One of the reasons Armentrout stands out to me compared to many other YA authors I read is the humor in her writing. It's sometimes dry, usually sarcastic, and always strategically placed. It's witty, not overly snarky, which I always prefer. Snarky usually comes off obnoxious--which I'm not a fan of--and even when there is snark, it's dry, jaw-dropping funny snark. All of it just makes the characters so believable and wildly entertaining.<br /><br />So...pretty sure I'm gushing at this point, so I'll stop. I'll end with mentioning my favorite scene and why I fell in love with Dawson and Bethany.<br /><br />I'll just call it the "reveal scene," when Dawson shares some information about himself that is pivotal in the story and in his relationship with Bethany. When he sees her reaction and closes the space between them and hugs her...holy crap. It's the sweetest scene and had me choking up because I could literally feel Dawson's relief and appreciation, the acceptance he needed. The whole scene was just so emotional and Bethany's inner monologue was so endearing.<br /><br />What can I say? Just read it, folks. Read the Lux series. If you love paranormal/sci-fi-ish romance, smartass characters, and fast-paced action, you'll love this gem and will be begging for more when it's over.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12318341448167628941" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_257073770" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/257073770" />
    <a title="Annie Brewer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5315988-annie-brewer"><img alt="Annie Brewer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442496062p2/5315988.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/257073770?book_show_action=true">Jan 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie Brewer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie Brewer" href="/user/show/5315988-annie-brewer">Annie Brewer</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=must-have-releases-of-2012">must-have-releases-of-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=irresistable-hot-guys">irresistable-hot-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=absolutely-amazingly-awesome">absolutely-amazingly-awesome</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=favorite">favorite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer257073770" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13208613323801314035">Gawd.....I love this series. I love Dawson and Daemon. I love Jennifer. Need to get my thoughts in order....review to come!<br/> <br/><br/>OKAY, I think I have had enough time to gather my thoughts so I can write my review for this. It wont be as long as my other reviews because I have so much to say but don't want to "spoil" anything for those that have not gotten to it yet! So here goes.....<br/><br/><br/>SO, yay!!! I was so glad to see Daemon and Dee again! I've especially missed Daemon like SO MUCH!!!!! Ever since I foun</span>
  <span id="freeText13208613323801314035" style="display:none">Gawd.....I love this series. I love Dawson and Daemon. I love Jennifer. Need to get my thoughts in order....review to come!<br /> <br /><br />OKAY, I think I have had enough time to gather my thoughts so I can write my review for this. It wont be as long as my other reviews because I have so much to say but don't want to "spoil" anything for those that have not gotten to it yet! So here goes.....<br /><br /><br />SO, yay!!! I was so glad to see Daemon and Dee again! I've especially missed Daemon like SO MUCH!!!!! Ever since I found out there was gonna be a novella about his TWIN brother, I had been itching to get my hands on it!! Boy were my hands itching like CRAZY!!! I was about to go to the doctor for some relief cream or something. But then I thought maybe my doctor would think I needed to see a psychiatrist instead. So, finally my hands stopped itching and all was good with the world.<br /><br />In the beginning we meet Dawson, Daemon's other half-sometimes better half, but not really. WOW, WOW, WOW, WOW, they are like SO different! Like night and day different. While Daemon is the arrogant prick, Dawson is the sweet and loving guy we all wish Daemon would be! But that's not true. I love Daemon even more after reading this. I mean seriously the things he suffers, OMG, my heart breaks for him!! I just want to jump into the book and hug him. I love his arrogant bantering(if that's the correct grammar) because he wouldn't be Daemon without it. Eventhough it would be a turn off if a guy pulled that shit in real life. But Daemon can totally tell me off anytime! <br /><br />We also meet Bethany, which okay she is AMAZING!!! Perfect for Dawson in every way imaginable. She is the new girl in school and walks into Dawson's class and it's like "Hello mama, come sit with me and I'll show you a whole new side of me no one has ever seen before" kind of thing. He is instantly drawn to her. I mean, I can't blame him. She is totally hot, sweet, kind and accepting of the most freakiest occurances ever! Of course I would be the same way with those HOT SEXY ALIEN GUYS too!! Damn, they are like electrifying! <br /><br />So, Dawson and Beth hit it off really well. He is the only one who actually talks to her, making her feel less like a loser being the new girl and all. They spend more time together and of course, Daemon and the rest of the Luxen clan are not to keen on the idea. The arum are lurking in the shadows of the small town of Fairfield. Dawson had already killed one in the beginning. So yea, they have a right to be paranoid about it. Not to mention the DOD are on their asses practically stalking them. It's nonsense, leave them alone already!!!! They creep me out!!<br /><br />Well, it takes a little time, but both of the love-sick puppies fall in love. It's so sweet and heartwrenching because we all know what happens!! She knows what he is but is like fascinated by it rather than scared. She reminds me of Katy more and more except she actually handled it better than Katy did, eventhough it was a lot for a human to process. *SIGH* I want Beth as my best friend!!! *tear*<br /><br />Even warning Dawson of the dangers, Daemon finally accepts that he has found the love of his life. I can see the pain and fear in Daemon for his brother's safety. Lighting up Bethany on more than one occasion like "the Fourth of freaking July" as Daemon put it, he still follows his heart!!! UGH, UGH, UGH....I've finally lost my train of thought. My tears are burning my eyes remembering the scene. Poor Daemon, poor Dee. Oh Dawson......no no no no no no no!!!!! My heart is splattered on the floor! I can't picture this, it's too much! My love for Daemon will never falter. Remember how obsessed I was? Geez, my review says it all. And I still feel the same way. But Dawson...oh DAWSON!!! God just his name brings those fluttery butterflies in my tummy!!<br /><br />Once again we see Ash, stupid mean bitch Ash whom I wanted to yank all her hair out!!! That is Katy's man, stay off of him!!!!!!!!!!!! *wishing he was mine* I don't get what Daemon sees in her, maybe just because they are both from the same planet I guess. Also, I did not like Andrew either. He was an ass. But wow, Adam.....he totally made me swoon when he stuck up for Dawson!!! Hell yes, Adam!!! You can rock my world too, there's plenty of me to go around baby!!!!!<br /><br />This book was riveting, compelling, mesmerizing, sexy, romantic, heartbreaking, sad, happy, suspenseful, page turning......EVERYTHING a YA book should be-even for a novella!! It was the best novella I've read! I want more!! The ending left me crying-real tears. I finished it in like 4 days because I couldn't bare the ending yet. All of my friends finished it before me because I was such a puss!! I knew what was coming! I had to brace myself and then take the plunge head on....it still didn't soften the blow though. UGH, UGH, UGH.......I hate having to wait for Onyx....and even worse since we have to wait 3 months more than originally planned!!! NO NO NO NO NO.....how will I survive this monstrosity!!!!!! I recommend reading this after Obsidian and I am glad I did because I understand everything better plus, it just makes sense to read Obsidian first!!! Oh Daemon. Oh Dee. Oh Dawson. Oh my heart. The end.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13208613323801314035" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

I'd find myself skimming so lines and skipping pages to get to a dialogue or something worth my attention. BUT by the end I was like wooooah there missy hold your horses, something is gana rock my world....and it did. <br><br>Dawson and Beth's love story was so cute, <b> "The FORBIDDEN LOVE" </b>, the kisses, them defending each other, Dawson always having her back, Dawson beating the crap -well almost- of Andrew and threatening him and Ash for even coming close to Beth... WOW!<br><br> <b> "Or what? Dawson spoke directly into Andrew’s thoughts, driving the point home. You <br> threaten Bethany again, in any way, and I’ll make sure you can’t talk again. To anyone. <br> Ever. Do you understand me? <br><br> “Dawson!” Ash yelled from below. “What are you doing? Stop! Do something, Adam!” Adam’s laugh followed. <br> “Someone needed to put Andrew in his place. I always figured it would be Daemon. Who knew.” </b><br><br>And Adam, let me say that I always feel that he's being neglected! But damn he's an amazing character! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ In the other books, he supported Dee's friendship with Katy. He stood with Daemon against his siblings when he declared his love with Katy. Damn he even got killed because of Katy and I know he'll do it again!!! I just know it. He has a great. loving, caring personalty that most people lack.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>I would be so honored to have him as a friend and a close one if I were Dawson, or Dee or even Daemon!<br><br><br>I regret not reading this before starting the LUX series, I would have known what Daemon was actually going through and why he hated Katy as a human in general and not as of her!!<br><br><br><br> <i>He kissed her deeply, holding her against him. When they broke apart the second time, his eyes were luminous and full of an emotion that sent her heart thundering against her ribs. Because she was sure she saw in his eyes what she felt.<b> Love. </b> </i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429523ra/860571.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_643241767" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/643241767" />
    <a title="☆ Sammy ☆彡" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14144676-sammy"><img alt="☆ Sammy ☆彡" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1462053159p2/14144676.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/643241767?book_show_action=true">Jun 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="☆ Sammy ☆彡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="☆ Sammy ☆彡" href="/user/show/14144676-sammy">☆ Sammy ☆彡</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13494685-shadows">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14144676-sammy?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14144676-sammy?shelf=young-adult-fiction">young-adult-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14144676-sammy?shelf=pnr-fantasy-horror">pnr-fantasy-horror</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer643241767" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4835430419815543330"><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[My heart hurts so freaking bad right now.. like I seriously want to cry! And it is even worse because I knew the ending was going to break my heart! Gah! <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><b>5 Stars!</b><br/><br/>*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*<br/><br/>This novella is a prequel to Obsidian, the first book in the Lux series. I don't want to give too much away, but this story is basically about forbidden love and the consequences that can occur. It is about a girl named Bethany, who moves to a new town where </span>
  <span id="freeText4835430419815543330" style="display:none"><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[My heart hurts so freaking bad right now.. like I seriously want to cry! And it is even worse because I knew the ending was going to break my heart! Gah! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>5 Stars!</b><br><br>*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*<br><br>This novella is a prequel to Obsidian, the first book in the Lux series. I don't want to give too much away, but this story is basically about forbidden love and the consequences that can occur. It is about a girl named Bethany, who moves to a new town where she meets Dawson, a handsome, charming, guy that is hiding a major secret. Can Bethany accept Dawson's secret? Will both of them be willing to fight for their relationship? What consequences will occur if they choose to be together? Shadows, a Lux novella, tells their story.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425649i/849634.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*<br><br>I actually read this novella out of order. I read Obsidian (Lux #1) first and am glad that I did so. Obsidian gives you a good understanding of the Luxen, their lifestyle, and their relationship with the human society. Without having that understanding, I would have been somewhat confused while reading parts of this novella (especially towards the beginning of the book).<br><br>I absolutely adored Bethany and Dawson <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[and I am hoping we haven't seen the last of them. I really hope they aren't dead and that the DOD lied about that :( <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> It was so interesting to see how different Dawson is from Daemon. Even though they are identical twins, they are polar opposites. While Daemon is constantly brooding, serious, somewhat antagonistic with others, and sarcastic; Dawson is charming, sweet, and an all around good guy. Don't get me wrong, I <b>LOVE</b> both of them, but it was fun to see how different they both are. <br><br><b>Overall,</b> I am loving this series so far. Which actually kind of surprised me because 1)YA isn't a genre that I read very often and 2)I avoid alien themed books/movies. I am so glad I decided to give this book series a chance because it is <b>SO FREAKING GOOD!</b> :)</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="4835430419815543330" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText3174543204022446584" style="display:none">This is the only book by JLA I don't like. At All. I don't like Bethany, I don't like Dawson and I don't like the plot.<br /><br /><b>Bethany</b> is just not my type of girl - girly, innocent, weak, damsel in distress-y. And honestly, how fucked up do you have to be to be okay with your BF being an alien in less than 5 minutes.<br /><br /><b>Dawson</b> was okay, though not as great as Daemon, until the point he fell in 'love' with Bethany. Even I, a hopeless romantic, would not be so selfish as to betray my family and friends and endanger my sister and brother. I would not even run away with y <i>one true love</i> whom I've known for a <i>month</i>. Plus, I <i>detest</i> selfish people, certainly those who kill themselves and leave their loved ones behind, which is practically what Dawson did since he <i>knew</i> it wouldn't, <i>couldn't</i> end well.<br /><br />The <b>plot</b> was very Twilight-y, cliché and really forced. I won't even put effort in writing up all the similarities to Twilight, since there are simply too much - the book is full of them. Also, all the dialogue war <i>been-there-done-that</i> and way too sappy. <br /><br />Lux and Covenant are two of my favourite series, but this book just made me heave.</span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer536454067271290193">I don't know what took me so long to get to this book considering that the Lux series is my absolute favorite but I'm so glad I did! I like Dawson in the main books but we really get to see how sweet, thoughtful, and protective he is. And I LOVED seeing Beth before everything that's happened to her, now I can really see how that altered her. Of course now I have to re-read the rest of it for the 20th or so time, so here we go😀 </span>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/550473702" />
    <a title="★★Sara Lizzy★★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17083195-sara-lizzy"><img alt="★★Sara Lizzy★★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1401476931p2/17083195.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/550473702?book_show_action=true">Mar 02, 2013</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer550473702" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15513781038060931573"><b>BR with Jo and Sammy</b><br/>(This was a re-read for me.)<br/><br/><b>5 Stars!</b><br/><br/><i>Shadows</i> is a prequel to <i>Obsidian</i> and tells the story of Dawson Black and Bethany Williams. This book also has in it Dawson's siblings, Daemon and Dee (they are triplets) as well as other supporting characters in the story. The story is told from Dawson's and Bethany's POV and occasionally Daemon's POV.<br/><br/>Dawson is a Luxen (an alien) and he falls in love with a human. <i>Shadows</i> is a novella about an instant attraction, a love that is frowned upon</span>
  <span id="freeText15513781038060931573" style="display:none"><b>BR with Jo and Sammy</b><br />(This was a re-read for me.)<br /><br /><b>5 Stars!</b><br /><br /><i>Shadows</i> is a prequel to <i>Obsidian</i> and tells the story of Dawson Black and Bethany Williams. This book also has in it Dawson's siblings, Daemon and Dee (they are triplets) as well as other supporting characters in the story. The story is told from Dawson's and Bethany's POV and occasionally Daemon's POV.<br /><br />Dawson is a Luxen (an alien) and he falls in love with a human. <i>Shadows</i> is a novella about an instant attraction, a love that is frowned upon by the Luxen community, problems Dawson and Bethany face when their love is criticized by some people in Dawson's family and his closest friends. And it's a story of what possible consequences and risks that a Luxen and a human face when they do fall in love and are in a relationship. I don't want to say more because it's such a short book and I don't want to give it away. I will tell you that you do <b>not</b> get a HEA in this novella.<br /><br />We read <i>Obsidian</i> first and <i>Shadows</i> second, even though that is out of order. The reason for that is because that's the way I had originally read the series the 1st time I ever read it, but also I've come across many people who read <i>Shadows</i> first and don't understand what is happening or don't get into the story because it's such a short novella that you don't really get a history of Luxen or Arum, so I always suggest that people read <i>Obsidian</i> first if you haven't read this series before. The only downfall to reading <i>Obsidian</i> before <i>Shadows</i> is that you are told what happens with Dawson and Bethany, so you will know what to expect in <i>Shadows</i> if you read them out of order, BUT if you read <i>Obsidian</i> first, you get a history of the Luxen and the Arum and will have a better understanding of the different alien races before you start <i>Shadows</i> which I personally think is best because it talks about Arum at the very beginning of <i>Shadows</i> and if you don't know what they are, then you may not appreciate the book or understand what is happening as well if you haven't read <i>Obsidian</i> first.<br /><br />Since I wasn't able to cover much in my review without giving anything away, here's a few of my favorite quotes from <i>Shadows</i>:<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Who knew West Virginia was hiding such hotness? If she'd known this before, she would've begged her parents to move here a hell of a lot sooner just for the eye candy.</i>
</b><br /><br />~~~~~~~~<br /><br /><b>"He stares at her like she's...." There was an odd pause, almost like Daemon really didn't know how to phrase it, as if he'd never stared at a girl that way before - and he hadn't. "Like she's the finest steak and he's starving."<br />Dawson's brows shot up. Was that how he stared at Beth? Like she was steak?</b><br /><br />~~~~~~~~<br /><br /><b>"I was outside, and it looked as if a light show was going on in your bedroom. Daemon said you were probably mas-"<br />And Dee also knew no boundaries.<br />"Ah, no, please don't finish that sentence." He lowered his hands, eyes narrowing on his sister. "Don't ever finish that sentence."<br /><br />~~~~~~~~<br /><br /><b>Instead of dumping his bowl and spoon like he normally did, he washed and dried them, setting them aside. Pivoting around, he darted his eyes back and forth between his siblings.<br />They stared openmouthed at him.<br />"What?" he demanded.<br />"Did you just....clean a dish?" Dee backed away slowly, blinking. She glanced at Daemon. "The world is going to end. And I'm still a vir-"<br />"No!" both brothers yelled in unison.<br />Daemon looked like he was actually going to vomit. "Jesus, don't ever finish that statement. Actually, don't ever change <i>that</i>. Thank You."<br />Her mouth dropped open. "You expect me to never have-"<br />"This isn't a conversation I want to start my morning with." Dawson grabbed his book bag off the kitchen table. "I'm so leaving for school before this gets more detailed."<br /><br />~~~~~~~<br /><br /><b><i>She. Spoke. To. Him. First. It was like winning the lottery, getting laid, and climbing the highest cliff all rolled into one.</i></b><br /><br />~~~~~~~~<br /><br /><b>She had no idea that he could literally stare at her all day. It was like he was obsessed. <i>Whipped</i> is what Daemon would say, but his brother didn't understand. Hell, Dawson wasn't even sure <i>he</i> understood what he was doing here, with this girl- this beautiful human girl.<br />This was trouble.<br />And he really didn't care.</b><br /><br />~~~~~~~~<br /><br /><b>"True love can conquer anything."<br />Her heart sped up as she glanced over her shoulder, meeting Dawson's gaze. He smiled, and she turned to mush.<br />"True love?" Daemon scoffed. "The entire concept of true love is stupid."<br />The class erupted in a debate that went way off topic, but Bethany and Dawson were still staring at each other. True love? Was that what this was? Before meeting Dawson, she would've been on board with Daemon's thinking. Now she believed in the gooey stuff.<br />Dawson's eyes deepened, turning a mosaic of greens.<br />Oh, yeah, bring on the gooey stuff.</b></b></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="15513781038060931573" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Erin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4979538-erin"><img alt="Erin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1520654483p2/4979538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/267661132?book_show_action=true">Jan 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Erin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Erin" href="/user/show/4979538-erin">Erin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">EVERYONE!</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer267661132" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12421026791409937035">Well, hello Dawson, so very nice to finally meet you!! This novella was an awesome short read, adding to what is already an awesome series!!<br/><br/>Dawson makes up one third of the Daemon/Dawson/Dee triplets, the beautiful alien siblings that live in a small town in West Virginia. In Obsidian we didn't get to meet him because he was already gone, either taken by the DOD or killed by the Arum. In Shadows, we get to hear his story, before that awful moment that still torments his family. <br/><br/>Dawson was so muc</span>
  <span id="freeText12421026791409937035" style="display:none">Well, hello Dawson, so very nice to finally meet you!! This novella was an awesome short read, adding to what is already an awesome series!!<br /><br />Dawson makes up one third of the Daemon/Dawson/Dee triplets, the beautiful alien siblings that live in a small town in West Virginia. In Obsidian we didn't get to meet him because he was already gone, either taken by the DOD or killed by the Arum. In Shadows, we get to hear his story, before that awful moment that still torments his family. <br /><br />Dawson was so much different from Daemon, which was really neat. I'm glad he wasn't just like Daemon, because well...there is no other Daemon!! Dawson was still hotness personified, but he was tender, sweet, and so completely in love with Bethany. He's drawn to her from the moment their eyes meet, but their romance doesn't just turn into some cheesy instalove. He spends time with her despite all of the warnings about what it could mean for their kind, because he can't deny his feelings. He falls hard for Bethany, and he's determined to keep her safe from the Arum and even his own kind. It's so sweet how he's so protective of her, and I couldn't help but gush! <br /><br />The ending gave us a little insight as to what happens to Dawson and Bethany that night, but of course not enough to know for sure where they are...dead or alive??? I have no doubts they'll be back, but the question is who has them...DOD, or the Arum (which is my theory...), and why??<br /><br />Oh, how I loved meeting 'little' brother Dawson and actually getting to see things from his POV!! I was so happy that Armentrout used both Bethany and Dawson's POV for this book, it always makes the story more exciting to hear what's going on in the guy's head, too! I will admit that the Daemon lover in me found it hard not to still pine for more Katy/Daemon action every time he came into a scene, but I knew going into this it would be a little painful in that department. Can't wait for August, when we'll FINALLY get to see them again in Onyx!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12421026791409937035" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer338522292" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5676737427370731344">This is one of the BEST prequels I've read. Not only is it a story all on its own, but the stupid cliffhanger ending left me screaming inside my own head. Surely, SURELY this can be explained!!! Surely, SURELY that did <b>not</b> just happen! What's sad is that I read Obsidian first, then realized that there was a prequel. So naturally I assumed that some of the unanswered questions I had regarding Bethany and Dawson would be answered. What this novella did was make me fall in love with them, and then </span>
  <span id="freeText5676737427370731344" style="display:none">This is one of the BEST prequels I've read. Not only is it a story all on its own, but the stupid cliffhanger ending left me screaming inside my own head. Surely, SURELY this can be explained!!! Surely, SURELY that did <b>not</b> just happen! What's sad is that I read Obsidian first, then realized that there was a prequel. So naturally I assumed that some of the unanswered questions I had regarding Bethany and Dawson would be answered. What this novella did was make me fall in love with them, and then leave me hanging. Urg! <br /><br />That being said (yelled, whatever...) I absolutely ADORED Bethany and Dawson. Dawson is Daemon's twin brother, but with a gentler demeanor. Bethany is the new girl in town. It's quite obvious almost immediately that they are fated to be together. The dual heartbeats are prevalent here. Their romance is sweet and spicy, and they are so comfortable with each other from the very start. You just KNOW that good things are to come from these two. And you just have to root for them, though the odds are obviously stacked against them. None of the Lux are on the side of their romance. Doom and gloom is around every corner.<br /><br />Another HUGE hats off to La La, who recommended this series. Its such an easy series to fall in love with. Seriously going straight to my favorites alongside Obsidian.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5676737427370731344" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText6860744137910947432" style="display:none">Shadows (Lux # .5) by Jennifer L. Armentrout <br /><br />Shadows in a short novella which fills in some blank spots about Daemons brother Dawson Black.<br /><br />Since I’ve read Obsidian (Lux #1) first this story gave me some of the unanswered questions I had about the missing brother and what may have happened to them.<br /><br />Even though this is a short story it is a great read, Dawson and Bethany are a great couple and I loved their story.<br /><br />If you’re a fan of Jennifer L. Armentrout writing this is a must read.<br />Shadows is about Dawson and Bethany how they met, the feelings, the romance, the acceptance of each other and oh did I mention hot boy. <br /><br />This short novel fills in some blank areas and you get to see how Dawson and Daemon are very different from each other but yet both swoon worthy. Best part is you get to read what happened to Dawson and Bethany and understand why they are not in Obsidian, the only question left is have they been taken by the DOD, are they dead? One can only hope they appear safe and sound…. This again is another must read!<br /><br />Jennifer has out done herself with this short novel and I have rated it another 5 star rating as I absolutely love her writing and the Lux Series. I recommend it to all my friends and followers.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6860744137910947432" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer245634097" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11112656923019014603">I simply couldn't resist reading this. I spent the entire morning NOT working. I'm bad, I know! But..but...it's Dawson and Daemon...and gah! <br/><br/>This gives us a background story as to what happened to Dawson and Bethany. We all know that they disappered without a trace prior to Obsidian, so no suprise as to the eventual ending of Shadows. I kind of half dreaded/anticipated reading this just for the very reason. I dreaded knowing Dawson's demise. At the same time, I think it was pretty cool to see wh</span>
  <span id="freeText11112656923019014603" style="display:none">I simply couldn't resist reading this. I spent the entire morning NOT working. I'm bad, I know! But..but...it's Dawson and Daemon...and gah! <br /><br />This gives us a background story as to what happened to Dawson and Bethany. We all know that they disappered without a trace prior to Obsidian, so no suprise as to the eventual ending of Shadows. I kind of half dreaded/anticipated reading this just for the very reason. I dreaded knowing Dawson's demise. At the same time, I think it was pretty cool to see what turned Daemon into the socially-inept, personality deficient that we've known of him now. He just went into an overdrive after his brother's "death". I am convinced that Dawson and Bethany didn't die. Unless I see their bodies, so to speak, I am keeping my hopes alive that they'll show up eventually. <br /><br />As usual, Ms. Armentrout gave me more than what I've expected. This little bitty is action-packed and brimming with funny and witty banters. Not gonna lie, I teared up on some occasions. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11112656923019014603" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17860217-trust-in-me"><img alt="Trust in Me (Wait for You, #1.5)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1376561229l/17860217._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('37dTclOKb3HaW+MYTNRCroPTn2wj48LLyg8HLlPnw/7lkTqg6NSmGX1wV3m7IUhxVYx4pO1uTKyRcUGfnqQxZA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }

It takes six years to slowly glue together the shattered pieces of her life, but Jillian is finally ready to stop existing in a past full of pain and regret. She takes a job at her father’s martial arts Academy and she’s going out on her first date since a failed relationship that was more yuck than yum. Jillian is determined to start living.\n\nShe just never expected Brock to be a part of her life again. But he’s firmly back in her life before she knows it, and not only is he older, he’s impossibly more handsome, more teasing and more everything. And when he sees Jillian, he’s no longer capable of thinking of her as the little girl who was his shadow growing up or the daughter of the man who gave him a second chance at life. He sees the woman who’d always been there for him, the one person who believed in him no matter what.\n\nBrock knows she’s the one he should’ve made his, and what begins as a tentative friendship quickly turns to red-hot chemistry that sparks a flame that burns brighter than lust. <span id="freeTextContainer12180507765886900548">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br/><br/>To email me, please use the below addy. <br/>jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br/><br/># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors yo</span>
  <span id="freeText12180507765886900548" style="display:none">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br /><br /># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors you’ve heard about her state aren’t true. When she’s not hard at work writing. she spends her time reading, watching really bad zombie movies, pretending to write, hanging out with her husband and her Jack Russell Loki. In early 2015, Jennifer was diagnosed with retinitis pigmentosa, a group of rare genetic disorders that involve a breakdown and death of cells in the retina, eventually resulting in loss of vision, among other complications. Due to this diagnosis, educating people on the varying degrees of blindness has become of passion of hers, right alongside writing, which she plans to do as long as she can. <br /><br />Her dreams of becoming an author started in algebra class, where she spent most of her time writing short stories….which explains her dismal grades in math. Jennifer writes young adult paranormal, science fiction, fantasy, and contemporary romance. She is published with Tor, HarperCollins Avon and William Morrow, Entangled Teen and Brazen, Disney/Hyperion and Harlequin Teen. Her Wicked Series has been optioned by PassionFlix. Jennifer has won numerous awards, including the 2013 Reviewers Choice Award for Wait for You, the 2015 Editor’s Pick for Fall With Me, and the 2014/2015 Moerser-Jugendbuch- Jury award for Obsidian. Her young adult romantic suspense novel DON’T LOOK BACK was a 2014 nominated Best in Young Adult Fiction by YALSA. Her adult romantic suspense novel TILL DEATH was a Amazon Editor’s Pick and iBook Book of the Month. Her young adult contemporary THE PROBLEM WITH FOREVER is a 2017 RITA Award Winner in Young Adult Fiction. She also writes Adult and New Adult contemporary and paranormal romance under the name J. Lynn. She is published by Entangled Brazen and HarperCollins.<br /><br />She is the owner of ApollyCon and The Origin Event, the successful annual events that features over hundred bestselling authors in Young Adult, New Adult, and Adult Fiction, panels, parties, and more.</span>
